(inDiviDоv)prоiсхоDit pо iх сubjекtu.В pеrvоm сluçае v gtоm каçесtvе vıсtupаöt госuDаrсtvа как tакоvıе,vо vtоrоm-фiziçескiе liüа (inDiviDı),t.е.tе,кtо nаprаvləöt i осuhесtvləöt госuDаrсtvеnnuö pоlitiкu,vırаcаöhuöсə v mеcDunаrоDnоm prесtuplеnii сооtvеtсtvuöhего госuDаrсtvа i оtvеtсtvеnnıе zа nее.ОDnако гlаvnım оbсtоətеlğсtvоm i оprеDеləöhim факtоrоm Dlə сосtаvа tакого prесtuplеniə əvləötсə prесtuplеniə фiziçескiх liü (inDiviDоv),322 коtоrıе pоluçili соvrеmеnnое nаimеnоvаniе «prесtuplеniə prоtiv mirа i bеzоpасnосti çеlоvеçесtvа».9.Так ili inаçе,соvrеmеnnıе mеcгосuDаrсtvеnnıе оtnоşеniə хаrакtеrizuötсə оprеDеlеnnımi izmеnеniəmi v сtоrоnu iх Dеmокrаtizаüii,nеоbхоDimосtğö кооrDinаüii i акtivizаüii uсiliy госuDаrсtv v соzDаnii nоvого mirо pоrəDка v rаzliçnıх оblасtəх соtruDniçесtvа i оtnоşеniy.İ есli bоlее ili mеnее оprеDеlеnnо mоcnо гоvоritğ оb iz vесtnıх pоzitivnıх rеzulğtаtах v соzDаnii nоvого mеcDu nаrоDnого gкоnоmiçеского pоrəDка,tо v оtnоşеnii nоvого mеcDunаrоDnого uгоlоvnого pоrəDка,оçеviDnо,çtо его фоrmirоvаniе tоlğко nаbirаеt сilu.В коnеçnоm сçеtе,uсiliə mirоvого сооbhесtvа v uсtаnоvlеnii nоvого uгоlоvnого prаvоpоrəDка согlасuötсə с коnüеpüiеy i Dокtrinоy соvrеmеnnого mеcDunаrоDnого prаvа v plаnе оbhiх uсiliy i соtruDniçесtvа госuDаrсtv pо rаzliçnım viDаm mеcDunаrоDnıх prесtuplеniy,v tоm çiсlе соvеrşеnnıх фiziçескimi liüаmi (inDiviDаmi).Воprос о privlеçеnii к uгоlоvnоy оtvеtсtvеnnосti gtiх liü zа vоеnnıе prесtuplеniə i Druгiе prесtuplеniə prоtiv çеlоvеçесtvа bıl оDnimi iz priоritеtnıх как pri vırаbоtке nоrm i pоlоcеniy Сtаtutа МУС,tак i v rеşеnii prоblеmı prогrессivnого rаzvitiə соvrеmеnnого mеcDunаrоDnого prаvа v üеlоm.10.Осоbıy nаuçnıy i prакtiçескiy intеrес prеDсtаv ləеt vоprос о öriсDiкüii МеcDunаrоDnого uгоlоvnого сu Dа i tо,как uсtаvı mеcDunаrоDnıх uгоlоvnıх tribunаlоv,utvеrcDеnnıе Соvеtоm Беzоpасnосti ООН,сpосоbсtvuöt rеşеniö gtоy vаcnоy prоblеmı.İtак,МУС,nесmоtrə nа tо,çtо его öriсDiкüiə nосit огrаniçеnnıy liçnосtəmi vо vrеmеni i prосtrаnсtvе хаrакtеr,əvləеtсə оDnim iz nоvеy şiх inсtitutоv mеcDunаrоDnого prаvа.ОçеviDnо i tо,çtо есli v оbоzrimоm buDuhеm Dеlо DоyDеt Dо соzDаniə rеаlğnого mеcDunаrоDnого tribunаlа,çtо,pо сuhесtvu,ucе сDеlаnо,Dlə сuDеbnого prесlеDоvаniə 323 liü,оtvеtсtvеnnıх zа сеrğеznıе nаruşеniə mеcDunаrоDnого гumаnitаrnого prаvа,соvеrşеnnıе v Афriке,Еvrоpе,nа Бlicnеm Восtоке,nа tеrritоrii Нагоrnого Каrаbаха,v ПriDnесtrоvğе ili еhе какоy-libо Druгоy «гоrəçеy tоçке»,pri vсех сuhесtvuöhiх nınе rеаliəх,tо «öгосlаvскiy»,«ruаnDiyскiy» prеüеDеntı как rеzulğtаt Dоlгiх uсiliy mirоvого сооbhесtvа v prесеçеnii i nеDоpuсtimосti löbıх prесtuplеniy prоtiv çеlоvеçесtvа,а tакcе nакоplеnnıy оpıt v gtоy оblасti buDut imеtğ,bеz prеuvеliçеniə,iскlöçitеlğnо pоzitivnое znаçеniе.İссlеDоvаniе nоrm i pоlоcеniy uсtаvоv соvrеmеnnıх mеcDunаrоDnıх uгоlоvnıх tribunаlоv,vкlöçаə,есtесtvеnnо,Рimскiy Сtаtut МУС,ucе imеöhiхсə rеzulğtаtоv iх Dеətеlğnосti pоzvоləеt сDеlаtğ vıvоD о tоm,çtо iх соzDаniе əvləеtсə сuhесtvеnnım Dlə rаzvitiə mеcDunаrоDnого prаvа i фоrmirоvаniə nоvого uгоlоvnого mirоpоrəDка.В коnкrеtnоm plаnе iх zасluга i Dосtоinсtvо zакlöçаötсə v tоm,çtо оni сpосоbсtvuöt uçrеcDеniö nоvıх mеcDunаrоDnо-prаvоvıх inсtitutоv i mехаnizmоv mеcDunаrоDnого prаvосuDiə,коtоrıе Dеyсtvоvаli bı nе tоlğко nа pосtоənnоy осnоvе (nаprimеr,МеcDunаrоDnıy uгоlоvnıy сuD),nо i оblаDаli bı univеrсаlğnоy öriсDiкüiеy,rасprосtrаnəöhеyсə nа vоеnnıе i Druгiе сеrğеznıе prесtuplеniə prоtiv mirа i bеzоpасnосti çеlоvеçесtvа.Чtо касаеtсə оtкrıtого i соziDаtеlğnого хаrакtеrа vnеşnеpоlitiçескоy Dеətеlğnосti АzеrbаyDcаnа nа соvrеmеnnоm gtаpе,tо оnа сvəzаnа с сеrğеznım uкrеplеniеm его сtrаtегiçескiх pоziüiy,с nаrаhivаniеm prакtiçеского i коnüеptuаlğnого pоtеnüiаlа gtоy Dеətеlğnосti,imеöhеy znаçеniе v коntексtе utvеrcDеniə pоziüiy АzеrbаyDcаnскоy Ресpubliкi nа mеcDunаrоDnоy аrеnе.Эtо осоbеnnо vаcnо i с tоçкi zrеniə pеrсpекtiv rаzrеşеniə zаtənuvşегосə nагоrnо-каrаbахского vооrucеnnого коnфliкtа,i rе-şеniə prоblеm rегiоnаlğnоy (каvкаzскоy)bеzоpасnосti,а tакcе rаzvitiə,uкrеplеniə i акtivizаüii соtruDniçесtvа 324 i pаrtnеrсtvа mеcDu vсеmi zакаvкаzскimi сtrаnаmi,осnоvаnnıх nа оbhеpriznаnnıх nаçаlах соvrеmеnnого mеcDunаrоDnого prаvа.11.Мnогоçiсlеnnıе,nо pока mаlоizvесtnıе факtı mеcgtniçескiх коnфliкtоv госuDаrсtv üеntrаlğnокаvкаzского rегiоnа pо сvоеmu соDеrcаniö,соvокupnосti i priznакаm vpоlnе охvаtıvаötсə öriсDiкüiеy МУС,pоскоlğкu v pоDоbnıх факtах priсutсtvuöt rаzliçnıе кvаliфiüiruöhiе glеmеntı,оprеDеləöhiе,v çасtnосti,vоеnnıе prесtuplеniə.ПосlеDniе,как скаzаnо v Рimскоm Сtаtutе,«соvеrşеnı v rаmках сооtvеtсtvuöhiх plаnоv pоlitiкi агrессivnıх сtrаn»,nаprimеr,оккupаüiə Аrmеniеy znаçitеlğnоy tеrritоrii АzеrbаyDcаnа,priznаnnаə v rеzоlöüiəх Соvеtа Беzоpасnосti ООН.В p.2 сt.8 Сtаtutа МУС оprеDеlеn хаrакtеr i uсlоviə сеrğёznıх prесtuplеniy (есtесtvеnnо,i vоеnnıх),а tакcе Druгiх prоtivоprаvnıх Dеyсtviy оккupаüiоnnıх сil,zа коtоrıе prеDuсmоtrеnı сооtvеtсtvuöhiе viDı mеcDunаrоDnоy uгоlоvnо-prаvоvоy оtvеtсtvеnnосti.Пriскоrbnо,çtо mеcgtniçескiе vооrucёnnıе коnфliкtı v üеntrаlğnокаvкаzскоm rегiоnе соprоvоcDаliсğ rаzliçnımi,i Dаcе izоhrёnnımi,viDаmi vоеnnıх prесtuplеniy (vо vсəкоm сluçае,pо tеm офiüiаlğnım Dаnnım,коtоrımi mı rасpоlагаеm pо Нагоrnоmu Каrаbахu),imеli хаrакtеr tакiх bоеvıх Dеyсtviy,как umışlеnnое nаnесеniе uDаrоv pо гrаcDаnскim оbjекtаm,zDаniəm,prеDnаznаçеn-nım Dlə rеliгiоznıх üеlеy,pо iсtоriçескim pаmətniкаm,mесtаm сосrеDоtоçеniə bоlğnıх i rаnеnnıх i Dr.İmеötсə tакcе mnогоçiсlеnnıе факtı i Dокаzаtеlğсtvа cесtокiх ubiyсtv ili rаnеniə liü,prinаDlеcаhiх к nеpriətеlğскоy nаüii ili аrmii,pосəгаtеlğсtvа nа çеlоvеçеское Dосtоinсtvо,iznасilоvаniе,priçinеniе uvеçiy,pıtкi i Dr.Воеnnıе prесtuplеniə v хоDе vооrucёnnıх коnфliкtоv,mеcDu какimi bı госuDаrсtvаmi üеntrаlğnокаvкаzско-го rегiоnа оni nе prоiсхоDili (pо кrаynеy mеrе,pо təcе-325 сti сvоiх pосlеDсtviy),mаlо v çёm оtliçаötсə оt Druгiх şirокоizvесtnıх vоеnnıх prесtuplеniy,vinоvniкi коtоrıх bıli сprаvеDlivо nакаzаnı pо uсtаvаm mеcDunаrоDnıх vоеnnıх tribunаlоv (Нörеnbеrгского,Токiyского i-оtnосitеlğnо nеDаvnо-pо bıvşеy Öгосlаvii i РuаnDе).ОDnако,nа nаş vzгləD,v nасtоəhее vrеmə,v оtliçiе оt соbıtiy pоluvекоvоy i Dесətilеtnеy Dаvnосti,nе оbəzаtеlğnо соzDаvаtğ nоvıе mеcDunаrоDnıе (vоеnnıе ili uгоlоvnıе)tribunаlı pо Нагоrnоmu Каrаbахu,Аbхаzii,Осеtii ili pо Druгim «гоrəçim» tоçкаm plаnеtı,гDе соvеrşаliсğ vоеnnıе prесtuplеniə.Нınе,i gtо Dосtаtоçnо оçеviDnо,çtо zа tакiе prесtuplеniə Dоlcnı nесti оtvеtсtvеnnосtğ vinоvnıе liüа v сооtvеtсtvii с pоlоcеniəmi i nоrmаmi vсtupivşего v сilu v 2003 г.Рimского Сtаtutа МУС,öriсDiкüiə коtоrого rасprосtrаnəеtсə i nа vоеnnıе prесtuplеniə,nеzаviсimо оt tого,гDе оni imеli mесtо.Есtесtvеnnо,nа vоеnnıх prесtupniкоv üеntrаlğnо-каvкаzского rегiоnа,согlасnо Коnvеnüii о nеprimеnimосti сrока Dаvnосti к vоеnnım prесtupniкаm i prесtuplеniəm prоtiv çеlоvеçnосti (1968 г.),nе mоcеt bıtğ pо iсtоriçескоy аnаlогii primеnёn сrок Dаvnосti.Соvmесtnıе cе uсiliə госuDаrсtv pо uгоlоvnоmu prесlеDоvаniö liü,соvеrşivşiх vоеnnıе prесtuplеniə,rегlаmеntiruötсə i mеc-DunаrоDnо-prаvоvım акtоm «Пrinüipı mеcDunаrоDnого соtruDniçесtvа v оtnоşеnii оbnаrucеniə,аrесtа,vıDаçi i nакаzаniə liü,vinоvnıх v vоеnnıх prесtuplеniəх i prесtuplеniəх prоtiv çеlоvеçесtvа»,prinətım Qеnеrаlğnоy Ассаmblееy ООН v 1973 г.,i Druгimi акtаmi,оblаDаöhimi сilоy mеcDunаrоDnıх zакоnоv.Такim оbrаzоm,mоcnо utvеrcDаtğ,çtо pоlоcеniə vışеprivеDёnnıх Dеyсtvuöhiх акtоv,v pеrvuö оçеrеDğ,Рimского Сtаtutа МУС,сосtаvləöt осnоvu mеcDunаrоDnо-prаvоvого mехаnizmа pо осuhесtvlеniö prаvосuDiə v оtnоşеnii liü,vinоvnıх v соvеrşеnii vоеnnıх prесtuplеniy i prесtuplеniy prоtiv çеlоvеçесtvа.326 12.Меcgtniçескiе vооrucеnnıе коnфliкtı госuDаrсtv üеntrаlğnокаvкаzского rегiоnа,bеzuсlоvnо,оblаDаöhiе priznакаmi коnфliкtоv mеcDunаrоDnого хаrакtеrа,vırаcеnnıе v сtоlкnоvеnii mеcDu vооrucеnnımi сilаmi prоtivоbоrсtvuöhiх сtоrоn,сpосоbсtvuöt pоrоcDе-niö vоеnnıх prесtuplеniy.СrеDi Druгiх priznакоv mоcnо vıDеlitğ оtnосitеlğnо огrаniçеnnıy tеаtr vоеnnıх Dеyсtviy i сrаvnitеlğnо nеbоlğşuö prоtəcеnnосtğ vо vrеmеni.Пri vсеm iх lокаlğnоm ili rегiоnаlğnоm хаrакtеrе,коnфliкtuöhiе vооrucеnnıе сilı оbəzаnı v сvоiх Dеyсtviəх соblöDаtğ сооtvеtсtvuöhiе mеcDunаrоDnо-prаvоvıе nоrmı,v çасtnосti,касаöhiесə zакоnоv i оbıçаеv vоynı,nе Dоpuскаtğ соvеrşеniə vоеnnıх prесtuplеniy,v tоm çiсlе pо gtniçескim mоtivаm,pоскоlğкu rассmаtrivаötсə как rаznоviDnосtğ prесtuplеniy prоtiv çеlоvеçесtvа,а znаçit i pоDpаDаöhiе pоD öriсDiкüiö оrгаnоv prаvосuDiə.İtак,mоcnо zакlöçitğ,çtо nınе сlоcilасğ tакаə сituаüiə,когDа nеrаvnоmеrnосtğ rаzvitiə rаzliçnıх сtrаn i rегiоnоv,prоtivосtоəniə,gкоnоmiçескiе i Druгiе кriziсı,i осоbеnnо gксtrеmizm,сеpаrаtizm i tеrrоrizm,сеrğеznо uгrоcаöt i rасşаtıvаöt mеcгосuDаrсtvеnnıе оtnоşеniə,соzDаöt кrupnıе prоblеmı pеrеD mirоvım сооbhесtvоm,его сuhесtvоvаniеm i uсtоyçivım rаzvitiеm.В сilu gtiх оbсtоətеlğсtv сlеDuеt оtmеtitğ,çtо löbаə bеzоpасnосtğ nеvоzmоcnа bеz соvmесtnıх mеcгосuDаrсtvеnnıх uсiliy,pоскоlğкu çlеnı gtого сооbhесtvа,как izvесtnо,rассmаtrivаötсə как осоbıе соüiаlğnıе əvlеniə i оrгаnizmı,оblаDаöhiе оprеDеlеnnımi vоzmоcnосtəmi v rеşеnii gtiх prоblеm.Пri gtоm rеçğ nе iDеt о tоm,çtо nаznаçеniе,nаprimеr,гlоbаlğnоy bеzоpасnосti Dоlcnо огrаniçivаtğсə vıcivаniеm çеlоvеçесtvа,ili nеоbхоDimо огrаniçivаtğ rоlğ mеcDunаrоDnоy bеzоpасnосti tоlğко zаDаçеy prеDоtvrаhеniə коnфliкtа.327 İСТОЧНİКİ İ ПРİМЕЧАНİƏ ВvеDеniе 1 Тексt сm.:Деyсtvuöhее mеcDunаrоDnое prаvо.В /3-х tt.Сосt.ÖМ.Коlосоv i ПоDrоbnее оb gtоm сm.,nаprimеr:ЭфеnDiеv О.f.МеcDunа-rоDnо-prаvоvое znаçеniе Рimского Сtаtutа МеcDunаrоDnого uгоlоvnого сuDа // ВоzrоcDеniе-XXI vек (Бакu),1999,сеntəbrğ,№ 19,с.70-76.359 Armed conflicts and war crimes in Central Caucasus:International law aspect Summary Present monograph has been dedicated to one of important problems of modern international law having practical value-the war crimes having been committed against the mankind.This problem runs essentially through the various,sufficiently intercommunicated and interdependent aspects of activities and interests of world community,such issues as international security,cooperation and partnership or the intergovernmental economic,social and humanitarian ones.Existing realities of international relations evidences that states committing crimes against the mankind does not observe provisions of international humanitarian law at the time of armed conflicts in which such states are involved.Therefore,an important place in the research is featured to the investigation of the UN activity,its respective bodies and units,in particular,in the sphere of rendering assistance to national efforts on averting armed conflicts and their grave consequences,restoration of supremacy of law in conflicting and post conflicted societies,etc.Thereupon,it is quite natural to accentuate on the provisions of Rome Statute of International Criminal Court (ICC).After it has come into effect ended the creation of systems of codified universal norms of international humanitarian (and criminal)law,which formed a kind of judicial "umbrella" above all other treaty commitments of the states dedicated to the struggle with serious crimes against the humanity.The international-legal analysis of this Statute has been realized by all-round consideration of its provisions.A particular attention in the research is given to the matter of criminal liability of physical persons,acting on behalf of the state and committing unlawful deeds qualified as war crimes.Preventing of any conflicts is one of the basic duties of sovereign states,which has been confirmed in particular in UN charter and other authoritative international legal instruments.Their interaction,efforts and partnership have to correspond to universally recognized principles and norms of contemporary international law.For ensuring the highest effectiveness of preventive measures they have to be brought about on more early stages of conflict.As regards with the aggravation of conflicts in Central Caucasus region,it had been engendered by the lack of experience-for their prevention in postsoviet space,and sometimes for inaction of international,regional and other organisations,including former central (soviet)government bodies.In the monograph come to light the main points and causes of conflict between Armenia and Azerbaijan,which have resulted in vast 360 disasters for the people of both countries.The author's consistent argumentation of his position testifies about the gross violations of universally recognized international legal norms and principles by Armenia,being confirmed in several present day authoritative,universal instruments and makes to come to a conclusion about the unlawfulness of the situation when the territory becomes the object of occupation by force of arms and violation of regulations of UN Charter.Peaceful settlement is featured as a key instrument of resolution of this conflict.While considering over the conflict in Abkhazia,which is rightfully regarded as one of the most bloodiest conflicts in the territory of the postsoviet Caucasus,are produced facts of ethnic cleansing / genocide,having been carried out by separatists against the Georgian population of Abkhazia and violation of territorial integrity of Georgia.Forcible demographic changes in the territory of Abkhazia being the result of armed conflict have been reflected in number of resolutions of the European Parliament,UN Security Council and recognized by number of OSCE sessions (Budapest,1994; Lisbon,1996).The conflict in South Osetia beginning at the same moment with the collapse of the USSR,revealed many unsolved problems connected with national-territorial demarcation and brought to light the reasons which have paved the way for local nationalism.Relative reduction of armed conflicts on the planet at the end of the XX century is considered by the author as a result of radical changes of balance of powers in the world in view of the collapse of bipolar system.With the collapse of the Soviet Union began to arise conflicts within postsoviet space.This circumstance requires the world powers and new sovereign states to keep in their development and interrelations practically and effectively not only the principles of political independence,but to respect such principles as sovereign equality,territorial integrity and other basic principles of contemporary international law as well.With regard to security in Central Caucasus,for the states,which the successful settlement of conflicts depends to a large extent on them (for instance,Russia,the US)the active neutrality,the balanced approach to the processes occurring here,is the most effective policy,which will contribute to formation of stable development in the region in the end.For all that,for the parties themselves fighting each other,having different points of view to the conflict settlement the unifying factor related to the creation of effective system for security here is the circumstance-that's the dynamic economic development,large-scale investments,mutually beneficial cooperation and partnership,a full-fledged integration of 361 Azerbaijan,Armenia and Georgia into the international community directly depend on the settlement of armed conflicts.At present,when the security of any state can be threaten by unilateral forced actions of other state the use of forces hasn't to be focused on changing of borders or territorial integrity.The conflicting parties must forbear from any aggression which may entail unjustified loses among the civilians or causal damages on civil objects.In the compensation of damages,being the result of any armed conflict,the vital importance has the regulations of Rome Statute of ICC,which have jurisdiction over the war crimes and aggressions as well.The norms,related to damage compensation at the result of armed conflicts arise not only from the imperative regulations and standards of international public law,but they have been aimed for the protection of common,material incentives of victims in such conflicts as well.Numerous,but not popular enough yet facts of conflicts in the region of Central Caucasus for their content,complexity and symptoms are fully covered by jurisdiction of the ICC,as far as there are different qualifying elements,defining in particular,the war crimes (capture of a sizable part of Azerbaijan by Armenia)being recognized in UN Security Council resolutions.In Paragraph 2,Article 8 of the ICC Statute there have been defined the character and condition of grave crimes (naturally,the war crimes too),as well as other unlawful acts of occupation forces,for which the international-criminal law makes provision for corresponding amenability.Armed conflicts in the region of Central Caucasus were accompanied by different,even highly refined war crimes.They have been characterized as military campaigns:delivering blows on civilian objects and buildings normally dedicated to religious use,historical monuments,places concentrated with sick,wounded and other people.There are also numerous facts and evidences for merciless murders or injury of people belonging to enemy party,grave breach of human dignity,rape,mutilation,tortures etc.For their after-effect heaviness the war crimes in the region of Central Caucasus in the course of armed conflicts differ a little from other analogical war crimes being worldwide known.The perpetrators of those crimes had been justly punished according to the Charters of International Court martial-Tribunals (of Nuremberg,Tokyo or relatively recent ones-on Yugoslavia and Ruanda).But,at present,unlike the 50 or 10 years standing events there is no necessity for new international tribunals on Nagorno-Karabakh,Abkhazia,Osetia or other "hot points" of the planet,where the war crimes have been committed.Perpetrators of such crimes must be called to account for the crimes they have committed in compliance with regulations and norms of Rome Statute 362 of the ICC having come into effect in 2003,jurisdiction of which can be applied to war crimes as well,irrespective where they have been committed.Naturally according to the Convention for inapplicability of the term of limitation to war criminals and crimes against humanity (1968)the term of limitation can't be applied on war criminals of the region Central Caucasus,on historical analogy.The join efforts of states in prosecution of persons having committed war crimes are regulated according to the international legal act "The Principles of international cooperation in regard with finding,arresting,extradition and punishment of persons who are the perpetrators of war crimes and the crimes against the humanity" adopted by UN General Assembly as far back as 1973 and other normative legal instruments having power of international acts.Thus,it can be proved,that the regulations of the above mentioned acts in force,in the first instance,the Rome Statute of the ICC comprise the basis of international law mechanism in restoration of justice in regard with persons who have committed crimes in Abkhazia,Nagorno-Karabakh and South Osetia.363 Окtаy ЭфеnDiеv
